 1
 For Internet radio station 'beats 1' will be completely free on radio

 It is more beneficial to include dry fruits in the diet than fresh fruits
 kyonki jo taaja fal aap kha rahe hai pataa nahin usamen aapaki jarurat ke mutabik sabhi vitamin or khanij shaamil hai yaa nahin
 Whereas in dry fruits all minerals are found according to your requirement
 isliye taaja fal kii jagah sookhe mewa zyada phayda karte hai
 Another special thing is that dry fruits can be kept for a long time and they can be taken anywhere
 sookhe mewa main taaje fal se zyada calories hoti he
 Three reasons for including dry fruits in the diet: According to research, it has been found that dried fruits are good sources of antioxidants
 jisase cancer, hriday rog, osteoporosis, madhumeh or mastishk jaisi kai bimariyon ke khilaaf ladane kii takat milti he
 Fiber: Dried fruits are believed to have more fiber than fresh fruits
 Fiber is necessary for our digestive system to function properly
 khubaani or kishmish jaise sookhe fal fibre ke achche strot hai
 Research suggests that fiber can also help prevent dangerous diseases such as obesity, heart disease, and cancer
 cholestrol / raktchaap:kaashew, baadaam, pista or kishmish jaise sookhe fal ek swasth sharir ke cholestrol ko control karne main madad karte hai
 It also helps in lowering blood pressure to a large level

 bina karj liye kheti karne vaale kisaanon ko bhi fasal beemaa se jodenge

 pehle iskaa data jari hua or jashn manaa ki naukariyaan milane lagi hai

 yani naukariyaan mili hai

 bijepi ne daawa kiya he ki kisaanon ko gehun ke liye 200 rupaya prati quintal bonus denge

 naveen fasal beemaa yojana laaenge jisamen fasal beemaa kii ikai khet rahegaa, jo kisaan swechha se isse alag rahanaa chaahate hai unhen anumati rahegi

 nai fasal aane ke purv fasal clem kaa vitaran karaayenge

 Farmers without taking loans will also be linked to crop insurance
 mandiyon main samarthan mulya se neeche fasal nahin bikne denge

 kisaanon ko upaj kaa nagad bhugtan teen din ke bheetar karenge
 ' karmchaaree bhavishyanidhi fund sanghathan EPFO ke aankadon main sanshodhan ke baad kaaphi kami ai he

 35 lakh nayaa panjikaran hua
 After the amendment it reduced to 29
 77 lakh par aa gaya he
 Ie 24
 4 pratishat kam ho gaya he
 Elections are being held in Madhya Pradesh on 28th
 battle ground ke tahat thodaa rajya kii sthiti kaa gauge lete hai
 The state is going to vote on 28th
 madhya pradesh main shivaraj singh chouhan chauthi baar mukhyamantri banane ke liye daavedaari kar rahe hai
 Elections are being held for 230 assembly seats in the state
 2013 main bijepi ko 165 siten mili thim
 72 percent of the population lives in villages of Madhya Pradesh
 28 fisadi aabaadi shahari maani jaati he
 Not only this, religious diversity is also very less
 91 fisadi aabaadi hindu maani jaati he
 7 percent are Muslim and 0
 3 pratishat isai
 20 percent belong to Scheduled Tribes and 15 percent belong to Scheduled Castes
 56 fisadi aabaadi gair anusuchit janajati or anusuchit jati kii maani jaati he
 According to the 2011 census in Madhya Pradesh, there are about 1 crore 54 lakh Scheduled Tribes
 vaise madhya pradesh ke janajaatiy kalyaan vibhaag kii website ke anusaar 46 prakaar kii anusuchit janajatiyaan hai
 It has the highest number of Bhil and Gond tribes
 inke baad vaiga, kol or sahariya aate hai
 In the Gond tribe, the Congress is considered more base
 2014 ke exit pole sample saise ke anusaar 60 pratishat gond congress main paksh main the lekin 37 fisadi bijepi ke
 Bhil tribe 58 percent in favor of BJP and 34 percent in favor of Congress
 ab chunaav kaaphi aage nikal chukaa he
 Nevertheless, the bsp's decision to fight alone remains on watch
 agar 2013 ke vidhansabha ke nateezon ko milakar dekhie to congress or basapa milakar chunaav ladati to donon ke paas 103 siten hoti
 The Congress then had 58 seats and the BSP 4
 agar yah gathbandhan hota to congress or bijepi ko 41 siton kaa laabh ho saktaa tha
 Especially in areas with scheduled caste influence
 kyonki madhya pradesh main 20 saal se basapa ko 6 se 9 pratishat ke bich miltaa hi rahaa he
 The highest was 9 percent in 2008 but 6 percent in 2013
 bijepi ne 39 pratishat tikat obisi ko or 24 pratishat tikat thakur ko, 23 pratishat brahman ko diya he
 Congress has also given 40 percent tickets to OBC, 27 percent to Thakur and 23 percent to Brahmins
 ye jaankaree hamane hindustan times main chhapi ek report se lee he
 Between 2003-2013, Congress has gained 6 percent in the Scheduled Caste area
 bijepi ne isi dauraan 1 pratishat kii badhottaree hasil kii he
 And the BSP has gained just 1 percent
 jabaki anya chote dal, nirdaleey ummidawaron ke paas 8 pratishat vot gaya he

 Madhya Pradesh is a rural state
 yahaan kisaanon kaa mudda kaaphi garam rahaa he
 Due to which Shivraj Singh Chauhan had to bring Bhavantar scheme related to procurement of crops
 bijepi ke ghoshnaa patr se hi pataa chalata he ki is yojana kaa laabh chote kisaanon ko nahin mila isliye unke liye alag vyavastha karne kii baat kahi gai he
 The Congress in its manifesto has said to withdraw the lawsuit filed against the farmers
 aaiye donon ke ghoshnaa patr se kuch baton ko jaldi se dekh lete hai
 The BJP has claimed that farmers will be given a bonus of Rs 200 per quintal for wheat
 jo duniya main kabhi bhi bina maange nahin diya gaya he
 An amount of 5,900 crore has been deposited in the account of 33 lakh farmers
 krishi vibhaag main karyaarat karmchaariyon or vaigyanik karmchaariyon kii sankhya ko doguna karenge
 Farmers will be encouraged to bring maximum agricultural land under scheduled crops under the Pradhan Mantri Crop Insurance Scheme
 nijee udyogon dwaara kharid patibaddhtaon or saarvajanik uparjan ke madhyam se vikrey dalhan kii 100 fisadi kharid sunishchit karenge
 100 new veterinary hospitals will be set up in 5 years
 5 saal main pashuon ke liye poli clinix kii sankhya 3 guni karenge
 Meteorological Corporation will be established
 mitti kii jaanch ke liye 1000 nae centre kii sthapana karenge or takniki karmchaariyon kii sankhya ko sunishchit karenge
 The comments congress ne apane ghoshnaa patr main likhaa he ki sabhi prakaar ke bainkon se liye gaye 2 lakh tak kaa karz maaf kiya jayega
 To give real benefit of the zero interest scheme to the farmers, the new date of payment will be kept till 31 May for the Rabi crop and 31 December for the Kharif crop
 pradhanmantri fasal beemaa yojana ko lekar congress ne kai prakaar ke badlaav pesh kiye hai
 New crop insurance scheme will be introduced in which the farm will be the unit of crop insurance, farmers who want to voluntarily stay away from it will be allowed
 beemaa compiyon dwaara kisaanon ko beemaa policy evam premium raashi kii raseed dena sunishchit kiya jayega
 They will distribute the crop claim before the new crop arrives
 gram sabha kii anushansa par fasal beemaa kaa laabh kisaanon ko denge
 We will amend the Land Revenue Circular 6-4 for compensation on crop losses of farmers deprived of crop insurance
 bina karj liye kheti karne vaale kisaanon ko bhi fasal beemaa se jodenge
 Crops will not be sold below the support price in mandis

 ' madhya pradesh main 28 taarikh ko chunaav ho rahe hai
 Let's take a look at the state of the state slightly under Battle Ground
 rajya main 28 taarikh ko matdaan hone vaala he
 In Madhya Pradesh, Shivraj Singh Chauhan is contesting for the fourth time as the Chief Minister
 rajya main 230 vidhansabha siton ke liye chunaav ho rahe hai
 In 2013, BJP got 165 seats
 72 fisadi aabaadi madhya pradesh ke gaanvon main rahati he
 28 percent of the population is considered urban
 yahi nahin dharmik vividhta bhi bahut kam he
 91 percent of the population is considered Hindu
 7 fisadi musalmaan hai or 0
 3 percent Christian
 20 pratishat anusuchit janajati ke hai or 15 fisadi anusuchit jati ke hai
 56 percent of the population is considered to be non-scheduled tribe and scheduled caste
 madhya pradesh main 2011 kii janaganana ke hisaab se kul 1 karod 54 lakh ke kareeb anusuchit janajatiyaan hai
 According to the website of Tribal Welfare Department of Madhya Pradesh, there are 46 types of Scheduled Tribes
 isamen bhil or gond janajati kii sankhya sabase adhik he
 They are followed by Vaiga, Cole and Sahariya
 gond janajati main congress kaa aadhaar zyaada mana jaataa he
 According to the 2014 exit poll sample size, 60 percent of the Gonds were in favor of the Congress but 37 percent of the BJP
 bhil janajati 58 pratishat bijepi ke paksh main or 34 pratishat kangrase ke paksh main
 Now the election has gone far ahead
 phir bhi basapa ke akele ladane ke faisle par nazar he
 If combined with the 2013 assembly results, the Congress and the BSP would have contested the elections, they would have had 103 seats
 tab congress ko 58 siten ai thim or basapa ko 4
 If it were an alliance, the Congress and BJP could have gained 41 seats
 khaskar anusuchit jati ke prabhaav vaale ilaake main
 Because in Madhya Pradesh, BSP has been getting between 6 to 9 percent for 20 years
 2008 main sabase adhik 9 pratishat mila tha lekin 2013 main 6 pratishat mila tha
 BJP has given 39 per cent tickets to OBC and 24 per cent to Thakur, 23 per cent to Brahmins
 congress ne bhi obisi ko 40 pratishat tikat diya he, 27 pratishat thakur or 23 pratishat brahman ko diya he
 We have taken this information from a report published in Hindustan Times
 2003-2013 ke bich anusuchit jati ke ilaake main congress ne 6 pratishat kii badhottaree hasil kii he
 The BJP has achieved an increase of 1 percent during this period
 or basapa ne sirf 1 pratishat badhat hasil kii he
 While other smaller parties, independents have got 8 percent of the vote

 The team of Prannoy Rai, Dorab Sopariwala and Shekhar Gupta spoke to Madhya Pradesh Chief Minister Shivraj Singh Chauhan
 madhya pradesh ek gramin rajya he
 The issue of farmers has been hot here
 jiske chalate shivaraj singh chouhan ko fasalon kii kharid se sambandhit bhavantar yojana lani padi
 bjp's manifesto itself shows that small farmers have not been benefited from this scheme, so it has been said to make separate arrangements for them
 congress ne apane ghoshnaa patr main kisaanon par daayar mukademe ko waapas lene kii baat kahi he
 Let us quickly see some things from both the manifesto
 bijepi ne daawa kiya he ki kisaanon ko gehun ke liye 200 rupaya prati quintal bonus denge
 Which has never been asked for in the world
 5,900 karod kii raashi 33 lakh kisaanon ke khate main jamaa kar di gai he
 Employees and scientists working in the Department of Agriculture will double the number of employees
 anusuchit fasalon ke tahat aane vaali adhiktam krishi bhoomi ko pradhanmantri fasal beemaa yojana ke tahat laane ke liye kisaanon ko protsaahit kiya jayega
 Will ensure 100% procurement of marketable pulses through purchase commitments and public procurement by private industries
 5 saal main 100 nae pashu chikitsaalay kii sthapana kii jaaegi
 In 5 years, the number of poli clinics for animals will be 3 times
 mausam vibhaag nigam kii sthapana kii jaaegi
 1000 new centers will be established for soil testing and technical staff will be ensured
 tippaniyan The Congress has written in its manifesto that the loan of up to 2 lakh from all types of banks will be waived
 kisaanon ko shunya byaaz yojana kaa vaastavik laabh dene ke liye bhugtan kii nai tithi rabi fasal ke liye 31 may tak kharif fasal ke liye 31 disambar tak rakhenge
 The Congress has introduced several types of changes regarding the Prime Minister's crop insurance scheme
 naveen fasal beemaa yojana laaenge jisamen fasal beemaa kii ikai khet rahegaa, jo kisaan swechha se isse alag rahanaa chaahate hai unhen anumati rahegi
 Insurance companies will ensure receipt of insurance policy and premium amount to the farmers
 nai fasal aane ke purv fasal clem kaa vitaran karaayenge
 On the recommendation of Gram Sabha, farmers will be given the benefit of crop insurance
 fasal beemaa se vanchit kisaanon kii fasal nuksaani par muawza hetu bhu rajasav paripatr 6-4 main sanshodhan karenge
 Farmers without taking loans will also be linked to crop insurance
 mandiyon main samarthan mulya se neeche fasal nahin bikne denge
 The farmers will be given bonus on wheat, paddy, jowar, millet, maize, soybean, mustard, cotton, pigeonpea, moong, gram, lentils, urad, garlic, onion tomatoes and sugarcane
 indira kisaan yojana ke tahat 10 harse power ke istamaal tak aadhi dar par bijli pradaan karenge
